{30001002|XXparameter|package|type request_type = 
record
  ascii string("\\0") request_url;
  record
    utf8 string("\\0") name;
    utf8 string("\\0") value;
  end[big endian integer(4)] request_url_params = NULL;
  void(big endian integer(4)) request_body = NULL;
end /* Metadata for records containing request information*/;
type response_type = 
record
  big endian integer(4) response_code;
  ascii string(big endian integer(4)) response_headers = NULL;
  void(big endian integer(4)) response_body = NULL;
end /* Metadata for records containing response information*/;

begin
  request.request_url :: "$\{URL\}";
  request.request_body :: in.__xx__request;
end;

begin
  out.__xx__response_code :: response.response_code;
  out.__xx__response_data :: reinterpret_as(utf8 string(big endian integer(4)), response.response_body);
  out.* :: in.*;
end;

begin

  error.error :: string_concat(error_info.error, string_concat(": ", (decimal(10)) error_info.error_code));
  error.* :: in.*;

{30001002|XXparameter|out_metadata|$[begin
  let pkg_info = package_info(in0_metadata);
  let dml_package_member[integer(4)] package_metadata_members = allocate();
  let dml_package_member[integer(4)] updated_members = allocate();
  let string(int) output_record_def = "";
  
  // ensure that the last member in our package is the metadata type declaration. older wsdl-to-dml
  // produce dml packages that end with type wsdl_generation_info 
  //
  // note we do not use vector_select and vector_difference as we care about order of members
  // 
  for (let package_member in pkg_info.members)
  begin
    if (package_member.form == "metadata")
      package_metadata_members = vector_append(package_metadata_members, package_member);
    else 
      updated_members = vector_append(updated_members, package_member);
  end

  // append the metadata to the end of the pkg_vec and put that back into pgk_info
  updated_members = vector_concat(updated_members, package_metadata_members);  
  pkg_info.members =  updated_members;
  
  // reconstruct a dml package with the metadata as the last element:
  output_record_def = make_package(pkg_info);
  
  // remove xml-to-dml generated types from the input
  begin block remove_xml_fields
    let expanded_record_def = expand_type(output_record_def);
    let expanded_record_def_info = record_info(expanded_record_def);
    let string(int)[int] fields_to_remove = [vector];    
    
    for (let record_def_info in expanded_record_def_info)
    begin
      if (record_def_info.name == "XML_namespace_mappings()")
      begin
        // the top level type is an xml-to-dml generated type, so replace
        // output_record_def with an empty record and exit the remove fields block
        output_record_def = "record\\nend;\\n";
        exit remove_xml_fields;
      end
      else              
        for (let field in record_info(record_def_info.dml_type))
          if (field.name == "XML_namespace_mappings()")
            fields_to_remove = vector_append(fields_to_remove, record_def_info.name);
    end
    output_record_def = remove_fields(output_record_def, fields_to_remove);
  end block remove_xml_fields
  
  // add the request field for the output from XML Combine
  output_record_def = add_field(output_record_def, "__xx__request", "utf8 string(integer(4))");
    
  result :: output_record_def;
end]|3|9||@{0|}}
